AuditWriter\n    38→\n    39→\n    40→class AuditTrailHelper:\n    41→    \"\"\"Wraps AuditWriter with auto-timer management for test convenience.\n    42→\n    43→    Each call to ``record()`` automatically starts the timer if not already\n    44→    started, ensuring ``duration_ms`` is always computable.\n    45→\n    46→    Attributes\n    47→    ----------\n    48→    writer : AuditWriter\n    49→        The underlying JSONL writer.\n    50→    results_dir : Path\n    51→        Directory containing the audit JSONL output.\n    52→    records : list[dict]\n    53→        In-memory list of all records emitted during the session.\n    54→    \"\"\"\n    55→\n    56→    def __init__(self, writer: AuditWriter, results_dir: Path) -> None:\n    57→        self.writer = writer\n    58→        self.results_dir = results_dir\n    59→        self.records: list[dict[str, Any]] = []\n    60→\n    61→    def start_timer(self) -> None:\n    62→        \"\"\"Explicitly start the timer for precise duration measurement.\"\"\"\n    63→        self.writer.start_timer()\n    64→\n    65→    def record(\n    66→        self,\n    67→        *,\n    68→        test_id: str,\n   verdict: str,\n    75→        evidence: str,\n    76→    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    77→        \"\"\"Write one audit record, auto-starting timer if needed.\n    78→\n    79→        Parameters match
